FROM [People] AS [p]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [l].[LandPropertyId], [l].[CadastralMark], [l].[Name], [l].[PersonId], [l].[Status], [t].[PlotId], [t].[CadastralMark] AS [CadastralMark0], [t].[DateOfSurvey], [t].[LandPropertyId] AS [LandPropertyId0], [t].[TotalAreaInHectares], [t].[LandTypeId], [t].[AreaInHectares], [t].[PlotId0], [t].[Type]

    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT [p0].[PlotId], [p0].[CadastralMark], [p0].[DateOfSurvey], [p0].[LandPropertyId], [p0].[TotalAreaInHectares], [l0].[LandTypeId], [l0].[AreaInHectares], [l0].[PlotId] AS [PlotId0], [l0].[Type]
